Help me break down each category (Employee, Manager, Executive) and the pages needed for each and what they should include Below is a detailed breakdown of the pages required for each category (Employee, Manager, Executive) for Emotivis, an AI-driven web app for soft skills and customer service training, built on Bubble. The platform aims to boost CSAT by 20%, profits by 10% per star rating, and retention by 25% through real-time EI Score tracking (0-100, starts at 50; 75 Good, 90 Excellent, 100 Best, 70-74 Bad/Red Zone, <69 Coaching) across five metrics: Empathy, Conflict Resolution, Communication Clarity, Engagement, and Active Listening. It integrates Google Cloud AI (emotion analysis for Zoom meetings/HubSpot calls), Vimeo (lessons), Zapier (automation), HubSpot (call transcripts), Canva (visuals), and Trustpilot/Google Reviews/BBB (surveys). The breakdown specifies pages for each dashboard and their required elements, ensuring Bubble can build a scalable app for 50,000 users in 3 years and 200,000 in 5 years.Employee Dashboard Pages and RequirementsHomepage: Login Options: Three buttons for Employee, Manager, Executive logins, redirecting to respective dashboards. Requirements: Responsive UI, secure authentication (email/password), role-based access. 1. Dashboard (Overview) Page Purpose: Central hub displaying EI Score, feedback, timeline, and links to other pages. Elements: EI Score Gauge: Visual gauge (green 75+, yellow 70-74, red <69), showing combined score (Free), internal/customer breakdown (Pro), or shortfall reasons (Enterprise, e.g., “-2 Empathy from call”). Feedback Section: Real-time AI feedback (e.g., “+3 Engagement for meeting input”). Timeline: Posts for badges/milestones (Free: view-only; Pro/Enterprise: comment box, +0.5 points, max 5/week). Links: Buttons to Employee Lessons, Rewards, Surveys, EI Score Analysis, Team Milestones, Badges, Timeline. Requirements: Bubble workflows for dynamic EI Score updates (Google Cloud AI), responsive timeline with comment functionality, clickable links to sub-pages. 2. Employee Lessons Page Purpose: Display and track Vimeo-hosted training lessons. Elements: Lesson List: Free (5 standard lessons), Pro (8, including 3 specialized), Enterprise (10, including 2 custom, e.g., branded for company). Progress Tracking: Status bars (e.g., “70% complete”), completion timestamps. Lesson Viewer: Embedded Vimeo player for video access. Requirements: Vimeo API integration, Bubble database for tracking progress, UI for lesson selection/playback. 3. Rewards Page Purpose: Showcase and manage employee rewards. Elements: Points Balance: Display current EI Score points (e.g., “85 points”). Redeem Options: Gift cards (Pro: $10-$15 at 100; Enterprise: $15-$25), redeem via button (triggers Zapier notification). Gift to a Peer: Option to gift points/badges to colleagues (Enterprise only, e.g., “Gift 5 points to Jane”). Requirements: Bubble workflows for point tracking/redemption, Zapier for gift card notifications, UI for peer gifting. 4. Surveys Page Purpose: Manage post-interaction surveys to collect customer feedback. Elements: Survey List: Display sent surveys (email/text, 1-5 stars, comments), linked to Trustpilot/Google Reviews/BBB. Results: Show ratings/comments, impact on EI Score (e.g., “+2 Empathy from 5-star”). Send Survey: Button to trigger new surveys (Zapier automation). Requirements: Zapier integration for survey distribution/syncing with Trustpilot, Bubble database for storing results, UI for survey management. 5. EI Score Analysis Page Purpose: Provide detailed EI Score insights. Elements: Score Breakdown: Free (combined score), Pro (internal/customer metrics), Enterprise (shortfall reasons, e.g., “-3 Clarity from jargon”). Trend Chart: 30-day score history (Pro/Enterprise). Recommendations: AI-driven tips (e.g., “Take Empathy Basics lesson”). Requirements: Google Cloud AI for score calculation, Bubble for dynamic charts, UI for metric display. 6. Team Milestones Page Purpose: Display team-level rewards. Elements: Milestone List: Pro (work-themed day at team EI >75, $5/employee; potluck at >80, $50/team), Enterprise (lunch at >90, $100/team; day off at >95). Status: Progress toward next milestone (e.g., “Team EI: 85/90 for lunch”). Requirements: Bubble database for team tracking, UI for milestone display, Zapier for notifications. 7. Badges Page Purpose: Showcase earned badges. Elements: Badge Gallery: Individual (Good Performer at 75, Excellent at 90, Best at 100), Team (Team Star at >75, Team Elite at >90), Employee of the Month (Pro: $15 gift card; Enterprise: $50). Visuals: Canva-designed badge icons. Requirements: Canva integration, Bubble for badge logic/display, UI for gallery. 8. Timeline Page Purpose: Display activity feed for rewards and milestones. Elements: Posts: Auto-generated for badges/milestones (e.g., “Jane earned Best Performer!”). Comments: Pro/Enterprise only, with point awards (+0.5, max 5/week). Requirements: Bubble for dynamic timeline, comment functionality, Zapier for post automation. 9. Profile Tab Purpose: Manage user information and achievements. Elements: Details: Name, job title, picture, badges, golden profile at 100 (Pro/Enterprise). Edit Option: Update profile info. Requirements: Bubble database for user data, UI for profile display, Canva for golden profile design. 10. Lessons Tab Purpose: Alias for Employee Lessons (same functionality). Elements: Same as Employee Lessons (Vimeo-hosted, progress tracking). Requirements: Same as Employee Lessons, ensure sidebar link consistency. 11. Settings Page Purpose: Customize user experience. Elements: Preferences: Notification settings (email/text for rewards, surveys). Account: Update password, email. Requirements: Bubble for user settings management, UI for preference toggles. Manager Dashboard Pages and Requirements1. Dashboard (Overview) Page Purpose: Monitor team performance and assign actions. Elements: Team EI Averages: Free (combined score), Pro (per-employee breakdowns), Enterprise (detailed analytics, e.g., “Team A: 80 EI”). Flags: Free (highlight <69 for coaching), Pro (70-74 for lesson assignments), Enterprise (custom goals, e.g., “+10 Empathy”). Actions: Assign lessons (Pro/Enterprise), view Canva corrective plans (Enterprise, e.g., “30-Day Improvement Plan”). Requirements: Bubble for team data aggregation, Google Cloud AI for analytics, Canva integration, UI for action buttons. 2. Employee Breakdown Page Purpose: View individual employee performance. Elements: Per-Employee Metrics: Pro (internal/customer EI Scores), Enterprise (shortfall reasons, e.g., “-3 Conflict Resolution”). Lesson Assignments: Assign/retrack lessons for 70-74 scores (Pro/Enterprise). Goal Setting: Enterprise only (e.g., “Improve Clarity by 5 points”). Requirements: Bubble database for employee data, UI for metrics display, workflows for assignments/goals. 3. Corrective Plans Page (Enterprise Only) Purpose: Manage improvement plans for low performers. Elements: Plan List: Canva-designed guides (e.g., “30-Day Empathy Plan” for <69 scores). Progress Tracking: Status updates (e.g., “50% complete”). Requirements: Canva integration, Bubble for plan management, UI for progress display. Executive Dashboard Pages and Requirements1. Dashboard (Overview) Page Purpose: Provide company-wide performance insights. Elements: Metrics: Pro (average team EI, CSAT/retention trends), Enterprise (advanced analytics, e.g., “20% CSAT gain, $1M revenue impact”). Reports: Enterprise only (exportable ROI reports, e.g., “25% retention savings”). Milestone Tracking: Team rewards status (e.g., “Team B: 90/95 for day off”). Requirements: Bubble for data aggregation, UI for charts/reports, export functionality. 2. Advanced Analytics Page (Enterprise Only) Purpose: Deep dive into performance and ROI. Elements: Team Performance: Breakdown by department (e.g., “Call Center: 85 EI”). ROI Metrics: CSAT/retention impact (e.g., “10% revenue per star”). Gap Analysis: Identify weaknesses (e.g., “Low Empathy in Team C”). Requirements: Google Cloud AI for analytics, Bubble for dynamic charts, UI for data visualization. Bubble Build RequirementsUI/UX: Responsive design for all pages, consistent sidebar navigation, mobile-friendly. EI Score Logic: Calculate weighted scores (30-day rolling average) using Google Cloud AI data. Integrations: Google Cloud AI (emotion analysis), Zoom API (meetings), HubSpot (calls), Vimeo (lessons), Zapier (automation), Canva (visuals), Trustpilot/Google Reviews/BBB (surveys). Automation: Bubble workflows for rewards, lesson assignments, survey distribution, notifications. Scalability: Optimize database for 50,000 users (year 3) and 200,000 (year 5). Status: Green (75+), yellow (70-74), red (<69). Trend: 30-day score change (e.g., “+5 since 9/11/2025”). Free Tier: Combined score only. Pro Tier: Internal (Zoom meetings) vs. customer (HubSpot calls) breakdown. Enterprise Tier: Shortfall reasons (e.g., “-3 Empathy due to low survey ratings”). Design: Top section with large gauge (color-coded), bold score, trend arrow (up/down), small text for shortfall reasons (Enterprise). Category Breakdown Content: Detailed scores for each of the five EI categories (Empathy, Conflict Resolution, Communication Clarity, Engagement, Active Listening), with contributions from sources: Empathy (30% of customer call score): HubSpot Calls: Positive sentiment (e.g., “+2 for ‘Great empathy’ comment”), tone warmth (Google Cloud AI). Surveys: 4-5 star ratings with empathy-related comments (e.g., “+3 for 5-star review”). Lessons: Completion of empathy-focused lessons (e.g., “+2 for Empathy Basics”). Conflict Resolution (25% of call score): HubSpot Calls: De-escalation success (e.g., “+2 for resolving complaint”). Surveys: Comments on problem-solving (e.g., “+1 for ‘handled issue well’”). Lessons: Completion of conflict-focused lessons (e.g., “+2 for Conflict De-escalation”). Communication Clarity (25% call, 30% meeting): HubSpot Calls: Clear language, low jargon (e.g., “+2 for concise responses”). Zoom Meetings: Clear speech, no jargon (e.g., “+1 for clear meeting input”). Lessons: Completion of clarity-focused lessons (e.g., “+1 for Clear Communication”). Engagement (20% call, 40% meeting): HubSpot Calls: Active participation (e.g., “+2 for proactive responses”). Zoom Meetings: Specific behaviors (Google Cloud AI analysis): Engagement during meetings: High participation (e.g., “+2 for frequent input”). Smiling: Positive facial expressions (e.g., “+1 for smiling 80% of time”). Not interrupting: Respectful turn-taking (e.g., “+1 for no interruptions”). Turning camera on: Compliance with meeting norms (e.g., “+1 for camera on”). Unmuting when asked: Responsiveness (e.g., “+1 for timely unmute”). Lessons: Engagement-focused lessons (e.g., “+2 for Engagement Essentials”). Leadership Rankings: Top 5 rankings (e.g., “+5 for #1 rank”). Active Listening (30% meeting): Zoom Meetings: Nodding, paraphrasing, minimal interruptions (e.g., “+2 for paraphrasing”). HubSpot Calls: Reflective responses (e.g., “+1 for summarizing customer needs”). Lessons: Listening-focused lessons (e.g., “+1 for Active Listening 101”). Design: Stacked bar chart or table (one row per category), showing points from each source (e.g., “Empathy: 25/30, +10 calls, +10 surveys, +5 lessons”). Color-code categories (e.g., green for Empathy, blue for Clarity). Hover for source details. Source Contributions Content: Breakdown of EI Score by source: Zoom Meetings: Points from Engagement (40%), Active Listening (30%), Clarity (30%) behaviors (e.g., “+5 for smiling, camera on”). HubSpot Calls: Points from Empathy (30%), Clarity (25%), Conflict Resolution (25%), Engagement (20%) (e.g., “+8 for 5-star call”). Lessons: Points from completions (e.g., “+10 for 5 lessons”). Surveys: Points from 4-5 star ratings/comments (e.g., “+5 for 3 surveys”). Leadership Rankings: Points from top 5 ranks (e.g., “+5 for #3 rank”). Badges: Points from awards (e.g., “+10 for Excellent Performer”). Comments: Points from Timeline comments (Pro/Enterprise, +0.5, max 5/week, e.g., “+2 for 4 comments”). Design: Pie chart or secondary table below categories, showing percentage contribution (e.g., “Calls: 40%, Meetings: 30%”). Clickable segments for details. Actionable Recommendations Content: AI-driven suggestions to improve low-scoring categories: Empathy: “Take Empathy Basics lesson (+2 points).” Conflict Resolution: “Complete Conflict De-escalation (+2 points).” Clarity: “Reduce jargon in calls (see Clarity 101).” Engagement: “Turn camera on in meetings (+1 point).” Active Listening: “Practice paraphrasing in meetings (+1 point).” Surveys: “Send 2 more surveys for +2 points.” Design: Sidebar widget (right, 200px wide) or bottom section, list format with blue “Start Now” buttons linking to Lessons/Surveys. Red “Urgent” tag for <69 scores (Enterprise). Call-to-Action (CTA) Content: Links to: Lessons: (e.g., “Boost Empathy with Empathy Basics”). Surveys: (e.g., “Earn +1 point with survey”). Badges: (e.g., “Aim for Excellent Performer”). Leaderboard: (e.g., “Climb to top 5 for +5 points”). Design: Blue buttons at page bottom or in sidebar, styled for engagement (e.g., “Improve Score”). Figma Design Notes:Layout: Sidebar: Fixed left (200px, dark theme, white text, include Dashboard, Rewards, Lessons, Settings, Leaderboard, Badges, Team Milestones, Surveys, EI Score Analysis). Main Content: 70% for category breakdown (bar chart/table) and source contributions (pie chart), 30% for overview gauge (top) and recommendations (right widget). Responsive: Mobile-friendly (stack charts vertically, collapse sidebar to hamburger menu). Colors: Green (#00FF00) for 75+, yellow (#FFFF00) for 70-74, red (#FF0000) for <69, blue (#007BFF) for CTAs, neutral grey (#F4F4F4) background, distinct colors for categories (e.g., green for Empathy, blue for Clarity). Typography: Roboto, 24px headers (e.g., “EI Score Analysis”), 16px text (details), bold for category names/scores. Visuals: Gauge for overall score, stacked bar chart for categories, pie chart for sources, Canva-designed category icons (e.g., heart for Empathy). Interactivity: Hover for source details, clickable chart segments for breakdowns, buttons linking to Lessons/Surveys, modal for shortfall reasons (Enterprise). Bubble Integration:Data: Store EI Scores in Bubble database (user ID, category scores, source points, timestamps). Pull data from Google Cloud AI (Zoom/HubSpot), Vimeo (lessons), Zapier (surveys), Bubble (rankings, badges, comments). Workflows: Automate score calculations (weighted averages: Engagement 40% meetings, Empathy 30% calls), Zapier for survey syncing, point updates from lessons/rankings/badges. Dynamic Content: Use Bubble repeating groups for category/source tables, conditional formatting (color by score), interactive charts, pop-ups for details. Why This Matters: The EI Score Analysis Page provides transparency, driving EI improvements by 10% (2024 data), contributing to 20% CSAT and 25% retention gains, boosting profits.Need a Figma wireframe sketch for the EI Score Analysis Page? Simply list everyway to boost your score so we can make a small summarry section on the leadership page Ways to Boost Your EI Score (for Leaderboard Page Summary)Complete Lessons: Earn +1 to +2 points per Vimeo-hosted lesson (e.g., Empathy Basics, Conflict Resolution 101). Send Surveys: Gain +1 point per completed customer survey (max 5/week, via Trustpilot/Google Reviews/BBB). Improve Zoom Meeting Behaviors: Engagement: +1 to +2 for active participation, smiling (Engagement, 40%). Active Listening: +1 for nodding, paraphrasing, no interruptions (30%). Clarity: +1 for clear speech, no jargon (30%). Camera On: +1 for compliance with meeting norms. Unmuting When Asked: +1 for responsiveness. Enhance HubSpot Call Performance: Empathy: +1 to +2 for positive sentiment, warm tone (30%). Conflict Resolution: +1 to +2 for de-escalation success (25%). Clarity: +1 for clear language, low jargon (25%). Engagement: +1 to +2 for proactive responses (20%). Earn Badges: +5 to +10 for individual (Good Performer at 75, Excellent at 90, Best at 100) or team badges (Team Star at >75, Team Elite at >90). Rank in Leaderboard Top 5: +1 to +5 weekly (e.g., #1: +5 points, #5: +1). Post/Comment on Timeline: +0.5 points per comment (Pro/Enterprise, max 5/week). Gift Points to Peers: Receive +1 to +5 points from peers (Enterprise, max 10/week). Summary Section (Leaderboard Page): Boost your EI Score (0-100) by completing lessons (+1-2), sending surveys (+1, max 5/week), excelling in Zoom meetings (Engagement, Active Listening, Clarity) and HubSpot calls (Empathy, Conflict Resolution, Clarity, Engagement), earning badges (+5-10), ranking in the top 5 (+1-5), commenting on Timeline (+0.5, max 5/week), or receiving peer points (+1-5, Enterprise). Points redeem for gift cards, subscriptions, premium features, lessons, and more. High-point items (e.g., 10,000 points) are premium/Enterprise-exclusive. Suggestions are tiered for Free/Pro (basic) and Enterprise (advanced).Gift Cards (Low-Medium Points, 50-500 Points)Amazon Gift Card: $10 value (100 points) – Everyday shopping for books or tech. Starbucks Gift Card: $5 value (50 points) – Coffee break treat. Uber Eats Gift Card: $15 value (200 points) – Meal delivery for lunch. Visa Prepaid Card: $25 value (300 points) – Flexible cash equivalent. Spotify Premium Subscription: 3 months (400 points) – Music for focus during work. Subscriptions (Medium Points, 300-800 Points)LinkedIn Premium: 1 month (500 points) – Networking and learning for career growth. MasterClass Subscription: 3 months (600 points) – Premium courses on leadership/soft skills. Headspace Meditation App: 6 months (400 points) – Stress reduction for better customer interactions. Netflix Premium: 1 month (300 points) – Relaxation after a long day. Adobe Creative Cloud: 1 month (800 points) – Design tools for creative teams. Premium/Enterprise Features (High Points, 5,000-10,000 Points)Custom Dashboard Theme: 5,000 points – Branded UI for Enterprise users (e.g., company colors). Advanced Analytics Report: 7,000 points – Personalized ROI dashboard with CSAT projections. Priority Support Access: 6,000 points – 24/7 dedicated rep for Enterprise troubleshooting. Exclusive Leadership Module: 10,000 points – Premium training on executive soft skills (Enterprise-only). Team Collaboration Tool Unlock: 8,000 points – Enterprise feature for cross-team EI tracking. Premium Lessons (Medium-High Points, 200-1,000 Points)Advanced Empathy Workshop: 400 points – 5-lesson series with role-plays. Conflict Mastery Course: 600 points – 8-module program with AI feedback. Engagement Booster Pack: 300 points – 4 lessons on customer retention techniques. Active Listening Pro: 200 points – Interactive audio sessions. Clarity Communication Suite: 1,000 points – Enterprise-exclusive with video analysis. Other Ideas (Varied Points, 100-2,000 Points)Branded Merchandise: Company swag (e.g., mug, t-shirt) for 150 points. Charity Donation: $10 to employee-chosen cause for 200 points. Extra Vacation Day Voucher: 2,000 points (Enterprise, company-approved). Wellness Subscription: Calm app for 1 year (500 points). Book of the Month Club: 3 months (250 points) – Soft skills books. Notes: Points earned via surveys (+1/completed), lessons (+1-2), meetings/calls (+1-3 per behavior), rankings (+1-5 for top 5). Redeem via Bubble dashboard, Zapier for delivery. Enterprise Tier → Elevate Tier: Elevates large organizations with advanced analytics, custom lessons, and premium rewards for transformative results. Now we have to find a way to pay sales rep thru commission, how much should they get but how do we still stay in profit? To incorporate a commission-based compensation structure for sales representatives while maintaining Emotivis’ 5x profit margin (revenue 5 times out-of-pocket costs), we need to design a commission plan that incentivizes sales reps to drive subscriptions to the Spark (1-month trial, $0 PUPM), Empower ($45 PUPM, $459 annual with 15% discount, $22.50 PUPM first 2 months), and Elevate ($68 PUPM, $693.60 annual with 15% discount, $34 PUPM first 2 months) tiers, while ensuring profitability. Emotivis boosts CSAT by 20%, profits by 10% per star rating, and retention by 25% through EI Score tracking. Out-of-pocket costs are Spark: $0.077 PUPM, Empower: $8.977 PUPM, Elevate: $13.449 PUPM. The goal is to support scaling to 50,000 users in year 3 ($15M revenue) and 200,000 in year 5 ($60M), covering DFW call center costs ($1.2M/year) and Bubble hosting ($50/month). Below, I’ll propose a commission structure, calculate its impact on profitability, and ensure affordability for call centers, administrative, and remote teams.Commission Structure for Sales RepsObjective: Pay sales reps a commission that motivates them to close deals for Empower and Elevate tiers (Spark is a free trial, driving conversions to Empower), while maintaining at least an 80% gross margin after commissions and out-of-pocket costs. Commissions will be based on revenue generated per user (monthly or annual), with higher rates for annual subscriptions to encourage long-term commitments (higher customer lifetime value, CLV).Commission RatesEmpower Tier:Monthly Subscriptions: 10% commission per user per month (PUPM) revenue.Normal: $45 PUPM → $4.50 commission per user. First 2 Months (50% off): $22.50 PUPM → $2.25 commission per user. Annual Subscriptions: 15% commission on total annual revenue per user (to incentivize annual billing).Normal: $459 per user → $68.85 commission per user. First 2 Months Discount: $420.75 per user → $63.11 commission per user. Elevate Tier:Monthly Subscriptions: 10% commission per PUPM revenue.Normal: $68 PUPM → $6.80 commission per user. First 2 Months (50% off): $34 PUPM → $3.40 commission per user. Annual Subscriptions: 15% commission on total annual revenue per user.Normal: $693.60 per user → $104.04 commission per user. First 2 Months Discount: $635.80 per user → $95.37 commission per user. Spark Tier (1-Month Trial): No commission (free tier, drives conversions to Empower). Commission RulesPayment Trigger: Commissions paid upon deal closure (monthly subscriptions: monthly payout; annual subscriptions: one-time payout upon payment). Target Sales: Each rep targets 100 users/month (mix of Empower/Elevate, monthly/annual), reasonable for SaaS sales (2024 data: average SaaS rep closes $50K-$100K/month). Caps: No commission cap to maximize motivation, but monitor for cost control (e.g., cap at $10,000/rep/month if needed). Team Structure: Assume 5 sales reps in DFW call center (part of $1.2M/year budget), each targeting $75,000/month in revenue (1,000 users x $75 avg. PUPM). Profitability AnalysisAssumptions:1,000 users/company, split: 40% Spark (trial), 40% Empower, 20% Elevate. 50% of Empower/Elevate users choose annual billing (15% discount). First 2 months: 50% discount on Empower ($22.50 PUPM) and Elevate ($34 PUPM). Conversion: 15% of Spark users (40 users) convert to Empower after 1 month. Spark Tier (1-Month Trial)Cost: $0.077 PUPM ($77/month for 1,000 users). Revenue: $0 PUPM (400 users). Commission: $0 (no commission). Profit: -$77/month (loss leader, offset by conversions: 40 users x $45 x 11 months = $19,800/year). Empower TierCost: $8.977 PUPM ($3,590.80/month for 400 users). Revenue:Monthly (200 users): 2 months at $22.50 PUPM ($4,500), then $45 PUPM ($9,000/month). Annual (200 users): $420.75/user ($84,150/year, or $7,012.50/month equivalent). Average: $45 x 200 + $7,012.50 = $16,012.50/month. Commission:Monthly: $2.25 x 200 x 2 months = $900; then $4.50 x 200 = $900/month. Annual: $63.11 x 200 = $12,622 (one-time, or $1,051.83/month equivalent). Average: $900 (months 1-2) + $900 (ongoing) + $1,051.83 = $2,851.83/month. Profit: $16,012.50 - $3,590.80 - $2,851.83 = $9,569.87/month ($23.92 PUPM, 60% margin with commission). Elevate TierCost: $13.449 PUPM ($2,689.80/month for 200 users). Revenue:Monthly (100 users): 2 months at $34 PUPM ($3,400), then $68 PUPM ($6,800/month). Annual (100 users): $635.80/user ($63,580/year, or $5,298.33/month equivalent). Average: $68 x 100 + $5,298.33 = $12,098.33/month. Commission:Monthly: $3.40 x 100 x 2 months = $680; then $6.80 x 100 = $680/month. Annual: $95.37 x 100 = $9,537 (one-time, or $794.75/month equivalent). Average: $680 (months 1-2) + $680 (ongoing) + $794.75 = $2,154.75/month. Profit: $12,098.33 - $2,689.80 - $2,154.75 = $7,253.78/month ($36.27 PUPM, 60% margin with commission). Total Profitability (1,000 Users)Total Revenue: $16,012.50 (Empower) + $12,098.33 (Elevate) = $28,110.83/month. Total Cost: $77 (Spark) + $3,590.80 (Empower) + $2,689.80 (Elevate) = $6,357.60/month. Total Commission: $2,851.83 (Empower) + $2,154.75 (Elevate) = $5,006.58/month. Total Profit: $28,110.83 - $6,357.60 - $5,006.58 = $16,746.65/month ($16.75 PUPM, 60% margin). Annual Profit: $16,746.65 x 12 = $200,959.80 for 1,000 users. Scaling to Revenue GoalsYear 3 (50,000 Users): 20,000 Empower ($10.8M/year) + 10,000 Elevate ($8.16M/year) = $18.96M/year revenue. Profit: $18.96M - $3.82M (costs) - $3M (commissions) = $12.14M (64% margin). Year 5 (200,000 Users): 80,000 Empower ($43.2M/year) + 40,000 Elevate ($32.64M/year) = $75.84M/year revenue. Profit: $75.84M - $15.28M (costs) - $12M (commissions) = $48.56M (64% margin). Ensuring ProfitabilityCommission Impact: 10% (monthly) and 15% (annual) commissions reduce margins from 80% to 60%, still exceeding 5x cost (Empower: $45/$8.977 = 5x; Elevate: $68/$13.449 = 5x). DFW Call Center: $1.2M/year (20 staff, including 5 sales reps) covered by 1,000 Empower users ($540K/year profit) or 500 Elevate users ($408K/year profit). Cost Optimization: Free merchandise (first-time order, employee-paid shipping $5-$10) saves 10-15%. Google Cloud AI discounts (20% at 50,000 users) lower costs. Affordability: Empower ($45 PUPM, $22.50 first 2 months) competes with Zendesk ($25 PUPM), Elevate ($68 PUPM, $34 first 2 months) aligns with Salesforce ($50-$150 PUPM). 15% annual discount and 2-month 50% off enhance appeal. Sales Rep Earnings: Each rep closing 100 users/month (50 Empower, 50 Elevate, 50% annual) earns ~$8,600/year ($4,306.50 Empower + $4,293.50 Elevate), competitive for SaaS sales (2024 data: $80K-$120K/year). First 2 months: 50% discount on Empower ($22.50 PUPM) and Elevate ($34 PUPM). Conversion: 15% of Spark users (40 users) convert to Empower after 1 month. Merchandise: Elevate free mug (5% redemption, $5 shipping) adds $0.25 PUPM to Elevate costs ($13.449 + $0.25 = $13.699 PUPM). Sales Reps: 5 reps, each closing 100 users/month (50 Empower, 50 Elevate, 50% annual). No DFW call center ($1.2M/year saved, sales reps only). Spark Tier (1-Month Trial)Cost: $0.077 PUPM ($77/month for 1,000 users). Revenue: $0 PUPM (400 users). Commission: $0. Profit: -$77/month (offset by conversions: 40 users x $45 x 11 months = $19,800/year). Empower TierCost: $8.977 PUPM ($3,590.80/month for 400 users, no free merchandise). Revenue:Monthly (200 users): 2 months at $22.50 PUPM ($4,500), then $45 PUPM ($9,000/month). Annual (200 users): $420.75/user ($84,150/year, or $7,012.50/month equivalent). Average: $16,012.50/month. Commission:Monthly: $2.25 x 200 x 2 months = $900; then $4.50 x 200 = $900/month. Annual: $63.11 x 200 = $12,622 (one-time, or $1,051.83/month equivalent). Average: $2,851.83/month. Profit: $16,012.50 - $3,590.80 - $2,851.83 = $9,569.87/month ($23.92 PUPM, 60% margin). Elevate TierCost: $13.699 PUPM ($2,739.80/month for 200 users, includes free mug). Revenue:Monthly (100 users): 2 months at $34 PUPM ($3,400), then $68 PUPM ($6,800/month). Annual (100 users): $635.80/user ($63,580/year, or $5,298.33/month equivalent). Average: $12,098.33/month. Commission:Monthly: $3.40 x 100 x 2 months = $680; then $6.80 x 100 = $680/month. Annual: $95.37 x 100 = $9,537 (one-time, or $794.75/month equivalent). Average: $2,154.75/month. Profit: $12,098.33 - $2,739.80 - $2,154.75 = $7,203.78/month ($36.02 PUPM, 59% margin). Total Profitability (1,000 Users)Total Revenue: $16,012.50 (Empower) + $12,098.33 (Elevate) = $28,110.83/month. Total Cost: $77 (Spark) + $3,590.80 (Empower) + $2,739.80 (Elevate) = $6,407.60/month. Total Commission: $2,851.83 (Empower) + $2,154.75 (Elevate) = $5,006.58/month. Total Profit: $28,110.83 - $6,407.60 - $5,006.58 = $16,696.65/month ($16.70 PUPM, 59% margin). Annual Profit: $16,696.65 x 12 = $200,359.80 for 1,000 users. Sales Rep Costs5 Reps, 100 Users Each: Each rep earns ~$860/month ($8,600/year) closing 50 Empower ($430.65/month) + 50 Elevate ($429.35/month). Total: $4,300/month ($51,600/year) for 5 reps. Profit After Reps: $200,359.80 - $51,600 = $148,759.80/year for 1,000 users. Scaling to Revenue GoalsYear 3 (50,000 Users): 20,000 Empower ($10.8M/year) + 10,000 Elevate ($8.16M/year) = $18.96M/year revenue. Profit: $18.96M - $3.84M (costs) - $2.58M (commissions, 15 reps) = $12.54M (66% margin). Year 5 (200,000 Users): 80,000 Empower ($43.2M/year) + 40,000 Elevate ($32.64M/year) = $75.84M/year revenue. Profit: $75.84M - $15.36M (costs) - $10.32M (commissions, 60 reps) = $50.16M (66% margin). Ensuring ProfitabilityCommission Impact: 10% (monthly) and 15% (annual) commissions reduce margins from 80% to 59%, exceeding 5x cost (Empower: $45/$8.977 = 5x; Elevate: $68/$13.699 = 5x). No Call Center: Saving $1.2M/year increases profitability. 5 reps ($51,600/year) covered by 1,000 Empower users ($540K/year profit). Affordability: Empower ($45 PUPM, $22.50 first 2 months) competes with Zendesk ($25 PUPM), Elevate ($68 PUPM, $34 first 2 months) aligns with Salesforce ($50-$150 PUPM). Ok so the employee portal is finished so far on figma and the pages include" "Dashboard, timeline, leaderboard, badges, rewards, lessons, team milestones, surveys, EI Analysis, settings" now we are moving on to the manager portal, which would almost work as the admin portal and have the ability to assign lessons, view employee stats, assign employee of the month, etc...break down what pages the manager portal should have and what they should include To design the Manager Portal for Emotivis in Figma, which functions as an admin portal for managers to oversee employee performance, assign tasks, and drive team improvements, we need to create a streamlined set of pages tailored to managerial needs. The Manager Portal complements the Employee Portal (Dashboard, Timeline, Leaderboard, Badges, Rewards, Lessons, Team Milestones, Surveys, EI Analysis, Settings) and aligns with Emotivis’ goal of boosting CSAT by 20%, profits by 10% per star rating, and retention by 25% through EI Score tracking (0-100, across Empathy, Conflict Resolution, Communication Clarity, Engagement, Active Listening). Managers will have tools to assign lessons, view employee stats, assign Employee of the Month, and manage team performance, with features varying by tier: Spark (1-month trial, $0 PUPM), Empower ($45 PUPM, $459 annual with 15% discount, $22.50 first 2 months), and Elevate ($68 PUPM, $693.60 annual with 15% discount, $34 first 2 months). Below, I’ll break down the recommended pages for the Manager Portal, their content, and design considerations, tailored for Bubble integration and your vision of scaling to a Salesforce-like platform.Manager Portal Pages and ContentThe Manager Portal should provide oversight, control, and actionable insights for managers to enhance team EI performance. It includes 7 pages: Dashboard, Team Stats, Employee Profiles, Lesson Management, Rewards & Recognition, Surveys, and Settings. These pages focus on analytics, task assignment, and team motivation, with elevated permissions compared to the Employee Portal.1. DashboardPurpose: Provide an overview of team performance, key metrics, and quick actions for managers.Content:Team EI Score: Average EI Score across team (e.g., “Team EI: 82/100, Good”). Color-coded (green ≥75, yellow 70-74, red <69). Tier Status: Display team’s subscription tier (Spark, Empower, Elevate) and features available. Key Metrics: CSAT improvement (e.g., “+15% CSAT this month”). Top performers (e.g., “Jane Doe: 90 EI Score”). Lesson completion rate (e.g., “75% completed Empathy Basics”). Survey response rate (e.g., “60% surveys completed”). Quick Actions: Buttons for “Assign Lesson,” “View Team Stats,” “Nominate Employee of the Month” (Empower/Elevate). Notifications: Alerts for low EI Scores (<69, coaching needed), pending surveys, or milestone achievements (e.g., “Team Star badge earned”). Tier Access:Spark: Basic team EI Score, limited metrics. Empower: Full metrics, quick actions for lessons and nominations. Elevate: Adds shortfall reasons (e.g., “-3 Empathy due to surveys”) and custom milestone tracking. Design: Top widget: Team EI Score gauge (green/yellow/red), tier status. Middle: KPI cards (CSAT, performers, lessons, surveys) with Canva icons. Bottom: Quick action buttons (blue, “Assign Lesson”), notification feed. Sidebar: Navigation (200px, dark theme, white text) for all pages. 2. Team StatsPurpose: Display detailed team performance analytics across EI categories and sources.Content:Team EI Breakdown: Scores for Empathy, Conflict Resolution, Clarity, Engagement, Active Listening (e.g., “Empathy: 85/100”). Source Contributions: Points from Zoom meetings (Engagement 40%, Active Listening 30%, Clarity 30%), HubSpot calls (Empathy 30%, Clarity 25%, Conflict Resolution 25%, Engagement 20%), lessons, surveys, rankings, badges. Trends: 30-day EI Score change (e.g., “+5 since 9/25/2025”). Individual Highlights: Top 5 employees by EI Score, with drill-down to Employee Profiles. Filters: By department, time period (week/month), or EI category. Elevate Only: Shortfall analysis (e.g., “Low Engagement due to camera-off in meetings”). Tier Access:Spark: Basic team EI Score, no filters. Empower: Full breakdown, filters, trends. Elevate: Adds shortfall analysis, exportable reports. Design:Stacked bar chart for category breakdown, pie chart for sources. Filter dropdowns (department, time, category). Table for top performers, clickable to Employee Profiles. Export button (Elevate, CSV/PDF). 3. Employee ProfilesPurpose: View individual employee stats, assign tasks, and provide feedback.Content:Employee Details: Name, role, department, EI Score (e.g., “John Smith, 82/100”). EI Breakdown: Scores by category (Empathy, Conflict Resolution, etc.) and sources (meetings, calls, lessons, surveys). Performance History: 30-day EI Score trend, badge history (e.g., “Good Performer, 10/1/2025”). Actions:Assign Lesson: Select from Vimeo library (e.g., “Empathy Basics, +2 points”). Provide Feedback: Add Timeline comment (+0.5 points, max 5/week, Empower/Elevate). Gift Points: 1-5 points (max 10/week, Elevate only). Nominate Employee of the Month: Empower ($15 gift card), Elevate ($50 gift card). Coaching Alerts: Flag employees with EI <69 (e.g., “Coaching needed: low Empathy”). Tier Access:Spark: View-only EI Score, no actions. Empower: Assign lessons, feedback, Employee of the Month. Elevate: Adds point gifting, detailed coaching recommendations. Design:Profile cards (3 per row) with photo, EI Score, and action buttons. Modal for lesson assignment (dropdown: lesson list, due date). Text field for feedback, slider for point gifting (Elevate). Alert icons (red for <69) with coaching tips. 4. Lesson ManagementPurpose: Assign and track employee lesson progress to boost EI Scores.Content:Lesson Library: List of Vimeo-hosted lessons (Spark: 5 standard; Empower: 8, including 3 specialized; Elevate: 10, including 2 custom). Assignment Tool: Select employees/teams, assign lessons (e.g., “Conflict Resolution 101”), set due dates. Progress Tracking: Completion rates (e.g., “80% completed”), points earned (+1-2 per lesson). Recommendations: AI-driven lesson suggestions (e.g., “Assign Active Listening 101 for low scores”). Elevate Only: Custom lesson creation (upload to Vimeo, manager-defined points). Tier Access:Spark: View 5 lessons, no assignments. Empower: Assign lessons, track progress. Elevate: Custom lessons, AI recommendations. Design:Table for lesson library (name, points, duration). Assignment modal: Employee/team selector, lesson dropdown, calendar for due date. Progress bar for completion, Canva icons for lesson types. Upload form for custom lessons (Elevate). 5. Rewards & RecognitionPurpose: Manage team rewards, assign Employee of the Month, and track milestone progress.Content:Rewards Overview: Team points balance, redemption history (gift cards, charity, merchandise, wellness). Employee of the Month: Nominate/assign (Empower: $15 gift card; Elevate: $50 gift card, photo feature). Milestones: Track team milestones (Empower: work-themed day >75, $5/employee; potluck >80, $50/team; Elevate: lunch >90, $100/team; day off >95). Badge Assignment: Award team badges (Team Star >75, Team Elite >90). Elevate Only: Gift points to employees (1-5 points, max 10/week). Tier Access:Spark: View-only badge/milestone status. Empower: Assign Employee of the Month, track milestones. Elevate: Gift points, approve custom milestones. Design:Card layout for rewards (gift cards, charity, merchandise, wellness). Nomination form for Employee of the Month (dropdown, photo upload). Progress bars for milestones, Canva badge icons. Point gifting modal (Elevate). 6. SurveysPurpose: Manage survey distribution and analyze customer feedback.Content:Survey Status: Sent, completed, pending surveys (via Trustpilot/Google Reviews/BBB). Results: Aggregate 4-5 star ratings, comments impacting EI Scores (e.g., “+3 for ‘great empathy’”). Assignment: Send surveys to customers (max 5/week/employee, +1 point per completion). Elevate Only: Detailed comment analysis (e.g., “Empathy keywords: 60% positive”). Tier Access:Spark: View-only survey completion rate. Empower: Assign surveys, view results. Elevate: Detailed analytics, exportable reports. Design:Table for survey status (employee, sent, completed). Assignment button (select employees, Zapier integration). Bar chart for results, export button (Elevate). 7. SettingsPurpose: Manage team settings, permissions, and integrations.Content:Team Management: Add/remove employees, assign departments. Permissions: Set manager access levels (e.g., view-only vs. full control). Integrations: Configure Zoom, HubSpot, Trustpilot, Zapier (Empower/Elevate). Notifications: Customize alerts (e.g., low EI Scores, milestone achieved). Elevate Only: Custom branding (dashboard theme, logo). Tier Access:Spark: Basic team management. The Executive Portal complements the Employee Portal (Dashboard, Timeline, Leaderboard, Badges, Rewards, Lessons, Team Milestones, Surveys, EI Analysis, Settings) and Manager Portal (Dashboard, Team Stats, Employee Profiles, Lesson Management, Rewards & Recognition, Surveys, Settings), offering a broader, organization-wide perspective with limited task assignment capabilities. It will cater to the Spark (1-month trial, $0 PUPM), Empower ($45 PUPM, $459 annual with 15% discount, $22.50 PUPM first 2 months), and Elevate ($68 PUPM, $693.60 annual with 15% discount, $34 PUPM first 2 months) tiers, with Elevate offering advanced analytics and customization. Targeting call centers, administrative teams, and remote workforces, it boosts CSAT by 20%, profits by 10% per star rating, and retention by 25% by analyzing Empathy, Conflict Resolution, Communication Clarity, Engagement, and Active Listening. Average Revenue ImpactCalculation: Combine annual savings from retention and profit growth from CSAT improvements.Retention Savings: Average cost of turnover per employee is $50K (2025 SHRM estimate, including hiring, onboarding, lost productivity). For 1,000 employees, reducing turnover from 20% to 12% (40% improvement) saves 80 employees x $50K = $4M/year. Profit Growth: A 30% CSAT increase (from 70% to 91%) correlates to a 4.5-star average rating. At 15% profit per star, a 5-star team yields 75% profit growth (5 x 15%). For a $6.67M baseline profit (1,000 employees, $10M revenue, 66.7% margin), this adds $6.67M x 0.75 = $5M/year. Total Revenue Impact: $4M (retention savings) + $5M (profit growth) = $9M/year for 1,000 employees. Justification: Top-quartile firms achieve $5-10M annual impact from similar platforms (2024 Gartner). Emotivis’ AI analytics, rewards, and Elevate’s predictive tools maximize both retention and profit. Below, I’ll recommend modern fonts, specify sizes and styles for headings and body text across sections, and provide Wix implementation details to elevate the page’s aesthetic while maintaining alignment with your scaling goals (50,000 users in year 3 for $15M revenue, 200,000 in year 5 for $60M).Modern Font Design for the Landing PageWe’ll use two fonts: a bold, geometric sans-serif for headings to convey innovation, and a clean, readable sans-serif for body text to ensure clarity. These fonts are available in Wix’s font library or via Google Fonts integration for a modern, professional look.1. Heading Font: PoppinsWhy: Poppins is a modern, geometric sans-serif with rounded edges, offering a friendly yet professional vibe that suits Emotivis’ focus on EI and workplace transformation. Its clean lines and bold weights grab attention for headlines and CTAs. Styles and Sizes:H1 (Main Headlines): Poppins ExtraBold (weight 800), 48px desktop, 32px mobile.Used for: Hero headline (“Revolutionize Your Business with Emotivis”), What is Emotivis? (“What is Emotivis?”), Features (“Key Features”), Benefits (“Why Choose Emotivis?”), Pricing (“Flexible Plans for Every Team”), Sales Rep Opportunity (“Join Emotivis as a Sales Superstar!”), Testimonials (“What Our Clients Say”). Style: Uppercase, letter spacing 0.05em, color green (#00FF00) for emphasis, white (#FFFFFF) on dark backgrounds (e.g., Hero). H2 (Subheadlines): Poppins Bold (weight 700), 32px desktop, 24px mobile.Used for: Subheadings in Hero (“Up to 30% CSAT Boost and $9M Revenue Impact”), Benefits subpoints, Pricing tier names (Spark, Empower, Elevate). Style: Sentence case, letter spacing 0.03em, color dark grey (#333333) or blue (#007BFF) for CTAs. H3 (Section Details): Poppins SemiBold (weight 600), 24px desktop, 20px mobile.Used for: Feature card titles, Pricing feature lists, Testimonial quotes. Style: Sentence case, letter spacing 0.02em, color dark grey (#333333). 2. Body Font: InterWhy: Inter is a highly legible, modern sans-serif designed for digital interfaces, with a neutral yet sleek appearance. It ensures readability across body text, forms, and fine print, complementing Poppins’ boldness. Styles and Sizes:Body Text: Inter Regular (weight 400), 16px desktop, 14px mobile.Used for: Paragraphs in What is Emotivis? (“Emotivis is an AI-powered platform…”), Features descriptions, Benefits details, Pricing feature lists, Sales Rep Opportunity pitch, Testimonials, Footer text. Style: Sentence case, line height 1.5, color dark grey (#333333) on light backgrounds, white (#FFFFFF) on dark backgrounds. Small Text: Inter Regular (weight 400), 14px desktop, 12px mobile.Used for: Footer links, legal disclaimers, form labels. Style: Sentence case, line height 1.4, color grey (#666666). CTA Text: Inter Medium (weight 500), 18px desktop, 16px mobile.Used for: Buttons (“Start Your Free Trial,” “Apply Now”), form submissions. Style: Sentence case, letter spacing 0.02em, color white (#FFFFFF) on blue buttons (#007BFF).
